PART W 24 
This Part reorganizes oversight and updates practices for serving infants, toddlers and 25 
children with disabilities from birth to 6 years of age. This Part: 26 
1.  Establishes the extended Part C option under the federal Individuals with 27 
Disabilities Education Act to continue individualized family service plans until the start of 28 
the school year when the child is 4 years of age if the family chooses; 29 
2. Provides that, beginning July 1, 2028, all school administrative units are responsible 30 
for child find activities and for ensuring a free, appropriate public education for children 31 
eligible under Part B, Section 619 of the federal Individuals with Disabilities Education 32 
Act; 33 
3. Provides that, until June 30, 2028, the Commissioner of Education is requi red to 34 
designate responsibility for child find activities and for ensuring a free, appropriate public 35 
education for eligible children to the Child Development Services System or to school 36 
administrative units in accordance with a transition schedule. Durin g the transition, the 37 
commissioner may approve school administrative units to assume the responsibility for 38 
child find activities and for ensuring a free, appropriate public education. The school 39 
administrative units must be provided professional learning and technical support and the 40 
department must assess and approve readiness plans. This Part adds to the duties of the 41 
director of early childhood special education within the department to support the 42

quarterly; 37

underserved through the Child Development Services System and establishes a review 43 
procedure for eligible children entering kindergarten or whose school administrative units 44

PART JJ 40 
This Part makes several changes to the laws governing the hospital tax. 41 
1 
2 
3 
4 
5 
6 
7 
8 
COMMITTEE AMENDMENT “B” to H.P. 1420, L.D. 2214 
Page 230 - 131LR3108(03) 
COMMITTEE AMENDMENT 
1.  It removes critical access hospitals from the definition of "hospital" beginning  1 
January 1, 2025. 2 
2.  It changes the tax imposed on hospitals from 2.23% to 3.25% beginning January 1, 3 
2025. 4 
3.  It specifies that the tax no longer applies to critical access hospitals beginning 5 
January 1, 2025. 6 
4.  Beginning January 1, 2025, it changes the taxable year for hospitals from 2020 to 7 
2022. 8 
5.  It clarifies that the changes beginning January 1, 2025 apply to the tax payment due 9 
on May 15, 2025. 10 
6.  It requires revenues received in each fiscal year from the hospital tax to be credited 11 
to the Medical Care - Payments to Providers Other Special Revenue Funds account to be 12 
used for MaineCare hospital payments. 13 
PART KK 14 
This Part requires an applicant seeking to convert a hospital into a critical access 15 
hospital to provide to the Department of Health and Human Services a copy of the 16 
applicant's most recent community health needs assessment, an estimate of the financial 17 
impact of converting to a critical access hospital and a utilization plan that includes the 18 
amount of total anticipated revenues that will be used and how they will be used to address 19 
the community health needs that are not being fully met at that time.  An approved critical 20 
access hospital must provide an annual report to the department for a period of 5 years 21 
demonstrating its use of revenues to support the health care needs of the community.   22 
Finally, this Part adds to the definition of "critical access hospital" a cross-reference to the 23 
new provisions of law enacted by this Part. 24 
PART LL 25 
This Part amends the laws governing reimbursement to critical access hospitals as of 26 
January 1, 2025 by terminating the requirement that the Department of Health and Human 27 
Services allocate to critical access hospitals for staff enhancement payments  at least 28 
$1,000,000 from hospital tax revenues collected under the Maine Revised Statutes, Title 29 
36, chapter 377 and $1,000,000 from hospital tax revenues collected under Title 36, chapter 30 
375. 31 
This Part also changes the reimbursement percentage to critical access hospitals from 32 
109% to 104.5% of MaineCare allowable costs beginning January 1, 2025. 33 
PART MM 34 
This Part requires the Department of Health and Human Services to ensure that 35 
aggregate MaineCare payments made to a group of hospitals comply with the uppe r 36 
payment limit applicable to that group as required under federal regulations. Beginning 37 
July 1, 2024, if aggregate MaineCare payments to a group of hospitals exceed the 38 
applicable upper payment limit, the department shall limit payments to that group to ensure 39 
compliance. The department must share its calculations and data related to the upper 40 
payment limit with affected hospitals at least 60 days prior to taking any action. 41

from the fund must be used to supplement, not supplant, other departmental expenditures. 32

certification as a behavioral health professional.  It requires the department to amend or 39 
establish contracts for training behavioral health professionals to train any number of 40 
additional individuals within existing resources and authorizes the department to opt to 41 
charge individuals or their employers fees for training. 42
